1935.09.09

Chairman Lin Returned to Beijing Yesterday Morning; Zhongshan Warship Docked at Naval Pier; President Wang and Others Welcomed Him at the Riverbank; Deeply Concerned About the Severe Disaster Situation Along the Way; Hoping People Will Work Together to Relief Disaster 1

(Nanjing) Chairman Lin, along with Lu Chao, Chen Xunyong, Mao Zhongfang, Xiao Qin, and others, arrived in Beijing at 9 a.m. on the 8th from Wuhu aboard the Zhongshan warship. Naval Commander Chen Shaokuan personally oversaw arrangements at the naval pier. The capital's police and gendarmerie dispatched officers to patrol the Jiangbian area in Xiaguan. The National Government sent a band and a guard of honor to wait at the pier. Central government officials who came to the pier to welcome him included President Wang, Zhu Peide, Ma Chaojun, Chen Zhuo, Chen Qicai, Wei Huai, and others, as well as representatives from various agencies and senior staff from the three departments of the National Government Secretariat, totaling about 300 people. The warship arrived at the heart of the river in Xiaguan at 9:10 a.m. The three warships, Hai Rong, Hai Chou, and Ying Rui, anchored on the river surface, fired salutes in respect. The band and guard of honor at the naval pier also played music and presented arms. Foreign ships all flew the Chinese flag to show their welcome. At 9:30 a.m., the warship docked at the naval pier. President Wang and other government officials boarded the ship in an orderly fashion to greet the Chairman and pay their respects. The Chairman received President Wang and the welcoming party in the reception hall, shaking hands with each one to express his gratitude. At 9:40 a.m., the Chairman disembarked and went ashore. Sailors on the Zhongshan warship lined up at the gangway, playing the national anthem to pay their respects. The welcoming party followed the Chairman off the ship. After disembarking, the Chairman traveled by car directly to his private residence at Shibanqiao to rest. According to the Chairman, in a conversation with reporters from the Central News Agency aboard the ship, he witnessed severe disaster along the way back from Lushan. The suffering of the victims was indescribable, and he was deeply concerned. Regarding the government's disaster relief measures, he had already discussed them with Kong during his stay in Lushan, dividing responsibilities for immediate and long-term relief efforts, which had already begun. He also dispatched Xu Shiying to inspect the disaster situation in various places to determine uniform standards for relief. He hoped that the people would work together to relieve the disaster. Huangshan's construction has made significant progress in recent years. He had originally intended to visit Qiaole Village to inspect the recent situation of returned overseas Chinese. The village even sent representatives to Wuhu to welcome him, but unfortunately, due to his desire to return in time to participate in the Central Government's commemoration of the first uprising led by Sun Yat-sen on the 9th, time did not permit it, so he did not go. He will visit them when he has time in the future. The Sixth Plenary Session has been postponed, so he has not yet prepared any proposals. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Yin Rugeng Arrived in Beiping Yesterday 2

(Tianjin) Yin Rugeng passed through Tianjin at noon on the 8th to go to Beiping, to meet with Shang Zhen and Takahashi to discuss the matter of the Northeast Special Police Force suppressing bandits along the Great Wall. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng arrived in Beiping this morning from Qinhuangdao. According to him, the situation was good during his inspection of places such as Yuguan and Qinhuangdao. Su Yuqi has been reinstated as Director of the Yu Public Security Bureau. He does not know whether the authorities are looking for a successor for the vacancy in the Ji-Mi District. He has ordered the staff of the public office to hand over everything at any time, and preparations are complete. The bandit situation is lighter in the Luan-Yu District. Bandits in the Ji-Mi District have also fled outside the pass, but as they flee out, others flee in, and the bandits' tracks are uncertain. The security team is strictly guarding against them. It may be possible in the future to realize the cooperation of the Japanese army outside the pass in suppressing the bandits at any time. He will not stay in Beiping for long, and after visiting Wang Kemin and Shang Zhen, he will return to Tangshan within a few days to inspect various counties. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Song Zheyuan's Inauguration Date Has Been Decided; Will Go to Beiping on the 14th of This Month to Take Office; Has Emailed Qin Dechun to Discuss Everything 3

(Beiping) The new Commander of the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison, Song Zheyuan, wired Qin Dechun yesterday, requesting that he go to Tianjin on the 10th to discuss Song's inauguration. Because Song has received telegrams from Chiang and He urging him to come to Beiping to take office as soon as possible, Zhu has decided to take office on the 14th of this month. According to a telephone call from Zhangjiakou, Qin, after receiving Song's telegram, has prepared to come to Beiping from Zhangjiakou tomorrow night, and then go to Tianjin to meet Song. After Song takes office, he originally intended to have the current Chief of Staff, Liu Jialuan, continue to serve as the Chief of Staff of the Beiping-Tianjin Garrison Command. However, Liu sent a telegram expressing his unwillingness to take the position, repeatedly begging Song to resign. Song's attempts to retain him were unsuccessful, and it was decided to appoint Chen Xiwun instead. Liu will be transferred to an important position within the department. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) Xiao Zhenying took a train to Beiping on the evening of the 8th to arrange everything for Song Zheyuan's inauguration. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Wang Kemin Hosted a Tea Party for the Press Yesterday; Reported on the Conclusion of the Beiping Political Readjustment Committee 4

(Beiping) Wang Kemin hosted a tea party for the press at the Political Readjustment Committee this afternoon. According to him, the Central Government had decided long ago to end the Political Readjustment Committee. After he received a telegram from the Prime Minister summoning him to Beijing for discussions, he returned to Beiping to handle the conclusion. Xu Xiuzhi, the commissioner appointed by the Executive Yuan to take over, will come north on the 11th and arrive in Beiping on the 13th. After the Political Readjustment Committee is handed over, he will go to Beijing in two or three days, and then to Hangzhou for a trip. Because his family is in Beiping, he will stay in Beijing for a week before returning north. The issue of placement of the staff of the Political Readjustment Committee is currently being addressed. Whether a custody office will be established in Beiping after the end of the Political Readjustment Committee will be decided after Xu Xiuzhi comes north. The Committee for the Preservation of Ancient Cultural Objects in the Old Capital will remain in Beiping, with the Ministries of Finance, Interior, Railways, and Education responsible. The engineering aspect will be the responsibility of the Mayor of Beiping. After the end of the Political Readjustment Committee, local diplomatic matters will be handled by the provincial and municipal governments. If the matters exceed the scope of the provinces and municipalities, they will be handled by the Central Government. The severance pay for the staff of the Political Readjustment Committee will be issued tomorrow. The severance pay for the advisors will be issued the day after tomorrow, after it is decided. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Tang Kesan Arrived in Beiping and Will Go to Suiyuan to Mediate the Incident of the Mantou Group Attacking the West Gong Banner 5

(Beiping) Tang Kesan, a member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, arrived in Beiping from Beijing at 1:24 p.m. on the 8th. It is heard that his mission this time, in addition to investigating the disturbances at the Mongolian and Tibetan schools, also includes going to Suiyuan within a few days to mediate the incident of the Mantou Group attacking the West Gong Banner. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Xu Bei; Dangerous Conditions Everywhere on the West Embankment; Shen Baixian Inspecting the Water Situation on the Central Canal; Breaching of the Bulao River, Enclosing It With a Levee 6

(Xuzhou) The west embankment and levee of Weishan Lake in Xu Bei are under pressure from the heavy Yellow River water. The water depth inside the embankment exceeds the supports, and it is seeping through in many places outside the embankment. Wutun, Yangchang, Taoyuan, and Zhengji are all located at the river mouth and are being inundated on both sides. The embankment is collapsing, and dangerous conditions are appearing everywhere. In addition to dispatching personnel to patrol the dangerous sections day and night, County Magistrate Wang Gongyu is personally patrolling day and night, urging the laborers west of the lake to raise and thicken the embankment. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

(Qingjiangpu) Su Jian's Director Shen Baixian, along with Xu Kai and others, took a boat north along the Central Canal on the morning of the 8th to inspect the water situation, passing through various key locations of the 360-zhang project in Huaiyin, instructing on protection strategies. He passed Zhongxing at noon and stayed overnight in Suqian. Regarding the county's defense, he believes it is connected to the Pi flood upstream and reaches Liutang on the side, and will conduct a special survey to determine the North Jiangsu Yellow River Defense Plan. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Xuzhou) After inspecting the breach on the south bank of the Bulao River yesterday, Shao Hanyuan today ordered the Sixth District to rush to block the Fangting River estuary, to build a levee around the breach, and to mobilize laborers from the Eighth and Ninth Districts to assist, with personnel dispatched by the county government to direct the work, starting construction immediately. Shao, considering the large number of victims from the 15 townships that have been affected, who have no homes to return to, ordered the districts east of Xuzhou to rush to take them in to avoid displacement. However, the people are eagerly awaiting relief. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Xuzhou) The Bulao River seized the mouth of the Fangting River, and the water rushed wildly, flooding and surging. The disaster area has expanded, and the entire eastern half of Xuzhou has become a lake. The south embankment of the Bulao River has completely lost its effectiveness. People and livestock have drowned, and the loss of grain and supplies is impossible to count. Occasionally, those who float out sitting in jars or holding onto wood take the railway subgrade as a temporary resting place. Food is scarce and relief is urgently needed. In addition, the county government has nowhere to impound ships, so many residents east of Xuzhou are in the water, waiting for rescue on rooftops and treetops. The disaster is unprecedented. In addition, the Longhai Railway passing through the water area east of Xuzhou is more than a hundred miles long. The roadbed east of the Daxujia station is level with the water, and many places have collapsed. Although three trains were allocated to transport stones to reinforce the line, some sections could not be reached. Starting on the 8th, trains will travel through the dangerous sections at a reduced speed. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

(Huaiyin) The Liutang River has surged, and the old Jingou gate in the Fifth District of Huaiyin has lost its effectiveness. The water has flowed backward towards the people's embankments and the Baojia River. The terrain in this district is the lowest, and it is about to become a disaster area. The county government has sent technician Liu Pingshi to rush to block the breach. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Huaiyin) Today, the water in Weishan Lake has risen by 3 centimeters, reaching 36.957 meters. The water in the Kiln has risen by 1 inch, reaching 225 inches. The water in Su has risen by 2 inches, reaching 188 inches. However, the mildewy water in the Inner Canal has not been completely discharged, which has attracted the attention of many doctors, who have put forward epidemic prevention opinions. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Xuzhou) The Lower Gate of the Inner Canal was closed to build a dam, blocking the waterway and diverting the Liutang River into the sea, causing the counties of Su and Pi to be in great danger. The Liutang River is both shallow and narrow, making it difficult to contain the fierce Yellow River water. Muyang has been desperately rushing to build embankments for days, and the embankments on both sides have overflowed. In addition, Pi County has been flooded by the Inner Canal and the Bulao River, and two-thirds of the county has been turned into a swamp. If the embankments in Xuzhou are not protected, then the entire Pi County will be submerged. The county is currently ordered by the Inner Canal Flood Prevention Office to build embankments, so it has no time for disaster relief. County Magistrate Qin Jieren has asked Commissioner Shao to appeal for relief on his behalf. Shao has ordered the rapid establishment of disaster relief shelters in various mountains and the use of warehouse reserves for disaster relief. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

The Yellow River Water Level Rises Sharply in the Wuyuan Area of Suiyuan 7

(Tianjin) A telegram from Suiyuan states that the Yellow River water level has risen sharply in the Wuyuan area. The Mu River canal has been breached, and the county town is in danger. They are currently rushing to block the breach. It is expected that if the water level stabilizes, the construction can be completed within a week. In order to assist with the construction, Fu Zuoyi has allocated a battalion of soldiers from Wang Jingguo's department to help with the work. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) A telegram from Suiyuan states that the weather in various counties of the province is exceptionally dry. Autumn weather is occurring in the summer season, and the harvest of crops has been greatly affected. Rice prices in the Wuyuan area have soared. Due to the rise of the Yellow River, drought and flood disasters have occurred simultaneously, and the people are in a state of panic. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Hutuo River Breached, Yunzhou Was Completely Flooded 8

(Tianjin) The Hutuo River in Renqiu County breached again on the 7th at the Li Guang Village and the west people's embankment of the North, South and West Three Cities in the Fourth District, a breach of two zhang. The water rushed out of the breach, directly pouring into the Miaotoup of Yunzhou, destroying more than 6,000 acres of farmland. The entire territory of Yunzhou was flooded, and all the villagers gathered on the dikes, trying their best to block the breach. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Water Level on the Eastern Section of the Longhai Railway is Rising 9

(Xuzhou) The water level on the eastern section of the Longhai Railway is increasing, and the Central Canal's discharge is insufficient. The railway line is extremely dangerous. The water level north of the railway is about to submerge the roadbed, and the people south of the railway are gathering to block the culverts, while the people north of the railway are planning to dig through the road to release the water. The special commissioner ordered the road protection teams organized by the Tong and Pi counties, after departing yesterday, to patrol back and forth and strictly prevent it. However, the discharge of the Central Canal cannot be delayed, otherwise the traffic on the eastern line will be interrupted. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Xuzhou) The Longhai Railway Bureau has specially dispatched the director of the Xuzhou office, Dong Yaotang, and the deputy director of the engineering department, He Gonghua, to be responsible for protecting the road and preventing flooding in the canal. According to He, the Tai-Zhao branch line has been abandoned, and efforts are now being made to ensure the safety of the main line, and to restore the Tai-Zhao line later. However, the official discharge of the Central Canal is insufficient, and it seems difficult for the water level to drop suddenly. The Daxu Station collapsed, and the roadbed is being filled. It is found that the water level in the Central Canal is level with the top of the embankment. Breaches have occurred at Mao'erwo and Guojiaokou. If the water level does not drop, it is feared that there will still be danger. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Construction of a Dam in the Upper Reaches of the Sanggan River Will Begin This Year 10

(Tianjin) As part of the fundamental treatment project for the Yongding River, three sand-blocking dams will be built in the upper reaches of the Sanggan River in Sanyuan County, Shanxi Province, at a total cost of 230,000 yuan. It has recently been approved by the Jinghui. The North China Water Conservancy Commission will organize an engineering team to depart this month for investigation, and construction will begin this year, starting with one dam. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Kong Xiangrong Talks About the Steps to Block the Breach at Dongzhuang 11

(Jinan) Kong Xiangrong said that blocking the breach at Dongzhuang will start with advancing from both sides, and finally throwing stones in the middle to close the breach. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Jiangsu Provincial Government Orders the Establishment of a Relief Branch in Xuzhou; Liu Datian Dismissed for Negligence in Flood Prevention 12

(Xuzhou) According to preliminary estimates by the county government, the Sixth and Ninth Districts east of Xuzhou, which were flooded by the Bulao River's Yellow River water, have more than 52,000 victims. All of their stored grain has been washed away, and no autumn crops have been harvested. The disaster situation in Pi County has been reported to be that two-thirds of the county has become a swamp, with approximately 300,000 victims eagerly awaiting relief. In addition, the Jiangsu Provincial Government recently ordered the Xuzhou authorities to quickly establish a Xuzhou branch of the Jiangsu Relief Association in order to take in the victims. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

(Xuzhou) Liu Datian, the head of the Sixth District east of Xuzhou, has been dismissed from his post by the special commissioner on the 8th for negligence in flood prevention, which led to the backflow of the Bulao River and the inundation of the Fangting River, causing a major disaster in more than 200 villages in the Sixth and Ninth Districts. He is still ordered to assist the newly appointed head, Li Bozhe, to quickly gather laborers to block and build dams at the estuaries of the Bulao and Fangting Rivers, and to enclose the water flow, and to work hard to provide relief to the victims in the water. The county government has ordered Yang Fang and Wang Shuren, the heads of the Eighth and Ninth Districts, to quickly gather a large number of laborers to rush to protect the southern embankment of the lower reaches of the Bulao River, to raise and thicken it to prevent further breaches. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Financial Authorities Plan to Raise Funds for Dredging Rivers 13

(Nanjing) The financial authorities, regarding the plan for a comprehensive solution to the problem of river flooding proposed by Kong Xiangxi, concerning the collection of funds for dredging, guiding, and returning wasteland to lakes and rivers, have been approved by the Executive Yuan in accordance with the original plan, and have been reported to the Central Political Council for record. Detailed implementation methods for raising these funds are currently being studied. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

The Typhoon Turns to Attack Southern Korea; Wind Forces in Shandong and the Yellow Sea Have Decreased 14

(Nanjing) According to the Central Meteorological Observatory, the typhoon reached the western sea area of Jeju Island at noon on the 8th, between 125.5 degrees east longitude and 33.5 degrees north latitude, proceeding due north. It has a tendency to turn and will land in southern Korea. The wind forces in Shandong and the Yellow Sea have decreased. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

(Qingdao) The hurricane struck Qingdao in the afternoon of the 8th. All ships were stopped, and the waves in the harbor were extremely large. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Tanaka Has Completed His Investigation of Inner Mongolia 15

(Beiping) According to a letter from Yuguan, Tanaka, a Japanese national investigating the industry in Inner Mongolia, has completed his investigation of the resources of eastern and western Mongolia in Chengde. Tanaka finished his work and left Chengde for Yuguan on the 6th of this month, inspecting the situations in Pingquan, Lingyuan and other places along the way. In addition, Matsui, the commander of the Japanese army unit stationed in Jin County, along with Lieutenant Colonel Horii, also arrived in Yuguan from Jin a few days ago and had some contact. Currently, Japanese nationals are frequently coming and going in Yuguan. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Bandits Raided Yi Yuan Pass, but Failed 16

(Beiping) According to a telegram from Yuguan, the bandit force of Wang Hong outside of Yi Yuan Pass once raided the interior of the pass on the 6th of this month. After the security captain Zhang Yantian dispatched the sixth and eighth companies of his troops, along with the Linyu public security team, to meet them head-on and suppress them, they were deadlocked until the morning of the 7th. The bandits were unable to withstand the pressure and fled to Damao Mountain, north of Yi Yuan Pass. Currently, security teams and police teams have been deployed to strictly guard Yi Yuan Pass, Guaizi Yu Pass and other places. More than 100 Japanese soldiers stationed in Suizhong County outside the pass also rushed to the vicinity of Yi Yuan Pass to assist in suppressing the bandits. In the battle of Yi Yuan Pass, a total of 83 bandits were killed and countless were injured. The bandit side suffered heavy losses. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) More than 300 bandits of the Yang and Er bandit gangs along the Great Wall line were still rampant on the 6th near Yuanhuashan, Kuoyuling, and Daguan. In addition, 400 to 500 bandits were entrenched in Weiyuzi, outside the Luo Wenyu Pass. The Zunhua militia has intensified its vigilance along the border wall. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) The bandits entrenched in Wen'an County were pursued and suppressed by the Tang Yongcai regiment of the Song Division of the 32nd Army. The remnants fled. The Tianjin-Zhan Security Command ordered the Tang regiment to clear the countryside in situ to eliminate the bandit scourge. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Wuhan Air Defense Exhibition Opened Yesterday 17

(Hankou) The military council's Wuhan Air Defense Exhibition Grand Assembly held a grand opening ceremony in Zhongshan Park on the morning of the 8th. Yuan Dakun delivered an opening speech on behalf of Presidents Jiang and Zhang. Jin Jutang reported on the preparations. Su Jilun, director of the Defense Committee, He Chengjun on behalf of Yang Senyi, and Zhang Qun on behalf of Wu Guozhen, and Ai Minying and Dan Chengyi of the Provincial and Municipal Party Committees spoke in succession, explaining the importance of air defense. During the meeting, five planes flew in the sky, distributing leaflets. The situation was extremely tense. After the meeting, the masses visited the exhibits. The exhibition rooms are located in the Liujia and Xinshichang areas, with a total of 22 sections, welcoming public visits. A film will be shown on the 10th to promote public awareness of air defense. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Director of the Chahar Construction Department Resigns 18

(Beiping) Zhang Weifan, Director of the Chahar Construction Department, recently resigned due to illness. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Guangdong Police Administration Observation Group Visits the Western Hills 19

(Beiping) The Guangdong Police Administration Observation Group visited various scenic spots in the Western Hills on the morning of the 8th. They are scheduled to begin visiting the municipal government's public security bureau and other agencies on the morning of the 9th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

The Beiping Finance and Printing Bureau Has Hope of Resuming Operations 20

(Beiping) The representatives of the workers of the Finance Ministry Printing Bureau who went to Beijing to petition telegraphed to Beiping, saying that the bureau has a hope of resuming operations recently, but the scope will be reduced. It is currently being reviewed with the Ministry of Finance, and they will continue to fight. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

The Beiping-Shanghai Through Train is Delayed Due to Flooding 21

(Beiping) The original arrival time of the Beiping-Shanghai northbound train was 10:24 a.m. every day. This morning, the train arrived in Beiping three hours late, not arriving until 1:24 p.m. The reason for the delay was flooding on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. (Special dispatch, 8th)

Otake Visits Military and Political Authorities in Beiping 22

(Beiping) Otake, the director of the Japanese special service agency stationed in Yuguan, came to Beiping from Yuguan last night. Today, he visited the military and political authorities of Beiping. He is scheduled to leave Beiping and return to Yuguan the day after tomorrow. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) Takeshita Yoshiharu, the director of the Japanese Kwantung Army's special service agency stationed in Shanhaiguan, came to Tianjin early on the 8th to visit Major General Tada and discussed the matter of cooperating in suppressing bandits along the Great Wall line. He took the night train to Beiping to meet with Military Attaché Takahashi for discussions. (Special dispatch, 8th)

(Beiping) Matsui, the military liaison officer of the Japanese Kwantung Army stationed in Zhangjiakou, arrived in Beiping from Tianjin this afternoon. He is scheduled to return to Zhangjiakou tomorrow. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Manchurian Gold Mining Company Refined 700,000 Taels of Gold in Six Months 23

(Tianjin) The Manchurian Gold Mining Company signed a patent mining right with the Puppet Ministry of Industry in Changchun on the 1st. The gold mines that the company has started mining are located in 20 places in Jilin and other provinces, and 80 places in Heilongjiang and other provinces. In the first half of this year, the company mined a total of 1.2 million taels and refined approximately 700,000 taels of pure gold. (Special dispatch, 8th)

The Tianjin Hydraulic Engineering Testing Institute is Scheduled to Open 24

(Tianjin) All preparations for China's first hydraulic engineering testing institute have been completed. The opening ceremony is scheduled to be held on the 11th. It is heard that the institute plans to have a very simple organizational structure, with one director in charge of various internal and external affairs, and a number of engineers in charge of testing work. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Wang Maogong Returns to Beiping from Tianjin 25

(Tianjin) Wang Maogong came to Tianjin a few days ago to visit Song Zheyuan and Cheng Ke on behalf of President Wang, and had some discussions. After completing his work, he returned to Beiping at 4 p.m. on the 8th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 8th)

Current Commentary

Prospects for British-Japanese Negotiations 26

— Xing

Great Britain considers the Far Eastern issue to be something that cannot be ignored, and that the deterioration of British-Japanese relations cannot be allowed to continue in a state of disorder for long. Therefore, it has dispatched Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, one of the foremost experts in its government, on a trip to the Far East, ostensibly to investigate China's economic and financial affairs, but in reality, he is tasked with resolving the East Asian disputes. Since Sir Frederick's departure, the Japanese press has been widely reporting that Sir Frederick's visit to Japan will involve discussions with the Tokyo government on dividing the Chinese market, opening the doors of the British dominions and colonies to accommodate Japanese goods, and resolving the disputes over naval issues and the crux of the problems in North China and Manchuria. Although the London government has repeatedly stated that Sir Frederick's mission is limited to investigation and recommendations and does not involve political negotiations, we observe the current state of British diplomacy and the attitude of the Conservative government, and the reports from Tokyo are not without reason. Matsudaira has returned to Japan, and Masuyama, the commercial counselor at the Japanese embassy in the UK, is also scheduled to arrive in Tokyo within a few days. Leith-Ross's trip, passing through Canada, arrived safely in Tokyo last week. This initial negotiation on adjusting British-Japanese relations is something we must pay attention to.

The gradual decline of British power in the Far East is the most important fact in Far Eastern relations since the European War. The rise of Japan in economic, military, and political terms has made it impossible for Britain to maintain its former dominance. After the September 18th Incident, it was followed by the dumping of Japanese goods in British territories. Although Britain resisted by raising tariffs and other methods, it has already shown many weaknesses. Geographically, militarily, and commercially, the current Britain is no match for Japan. Britain's problem is only how to preserve its existing rights and interests, so that its Far Eastern power, which has been painstakingly built over decades, will not dissipate completely. Japan's hope is to monopolize the Far East. Britain's hope is only to maintain a certain sphere of influence. Therefore, observing the current trend, if Japan makes slight concessions, Britain, for the sake of future security, will not hesitate to use the Chinese market as a bargaining chip. Today, Japan not only wants to incorporate North China into its economic sphere of influence, but is also gradually seeking to drive the British out of Hong Kong or south of Singapore. What Leith-Ross can do is, at most, only to slightly alleviate Japan's encroachment on Britain's existing rights and interests in the Far East and India, or to guide Japan's expansion in a certain direction to reduce the losses suffered by Britain. If we hope to use the power of Britain to prevent Japan's encroachment in China, it is simply wishful thinking.

According to reports, the basic policy of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs for negotiations with Britain includes items such as "Britain should open its world territories to Japan" and "Britain must not prevent Japan's development in Manchuria and China." This is not Japan's boast, but the true hope of the Japanese government. For several days, Japanese newspapers have been full of warnings to Britain, such as demanding that Britain hand over the Chinese customs administration and reform the Shanghai Municipal Council. The arrogance is overwhelming. However, Japan has economic and military power as its backing. Those pragmatic British are accustomed to enduring things. Within certain limits, Britain will not hesitate to sacrifice the prestige of white people in the Far East in order to preserve its substantial interests. Moreover, the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia has reached the point of explosion. Once Britain is drawn into the vortex, it will have no energy to spare for the Far East. Britain's planes and warships are limited, while Japan's desires are endless. The day the war breaks out in the Red Sea and the Mediterranean is the day Japan's military will extend into Hong Kong, Singapore, and India. If Britain does not compromise with Japan now and entice it with substantial benefits, then the area west of the Suez will inevitably be touched by Japan when Britain is occupied in Europe and Africa. Moreover, Australia, New Ceylon, and other areas have long been coveted by Japan. Britain has no power to look east and has failed to cooperate effectively with the United States. The possibility of Japan's expansion is unknown.

Therefore, the Tokyo negotiations will inevitably increase in difficulty due to the tension in the African situation. The more difficult the situation in Europe, the stronger Japan's attitude will be, and the more likely Britain will yield. Leith-Ross unfortunately arrived in Tokyo when the Italian-Abyssinian War was imminent. China unfortunately has negotiations on economic cooperation in North China at the time of Leith-Ross's arrival in Japan. Looking at the current situation, British power in the Far East is difficult to avoid declining, and our country's situation is even more dangerous. Can those who hold the reins of power not be cautious and careful in their handling of affairs, so as to overcome the current difficulties?

Puyi Arrives in Harbin 27

(Harbin) Puyi arrived here this afternoon from Changchun by train. The commander of the Kwantung Leased Territory, General Minami, welcomed him. After Puyi got off the train, he greeted the crowd and left the station by car, escorted by cavalry. There were many onlookers along the way. If the weather is fine, Puyi will inspect the Songhua River Fleet tomorrow. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs: Northeast Immigration Plan, Establishing a Company with 15 Million in Capital 28

(Tokyo) The Overseas Colonial Affairs Committee of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs dispatched Director General of the Colonial Affairs Bureau, Mr. Takayama, to inspect the current state of agricultural immigration in Manchuria. He has now completed his inspection and returned to Tokyo. A general meeting is scheduled to be held at the Minister's official residence on the 10th of this month. This meeting will establish a national policy for the long-pending Manchurian immigration project, aiming for its realization. The plan is to initiate the project in the next fiscal year, abandoning the initial grand colonial company plan and establishing only an immigration company with capital of approximately 15 million yuan. The company will provide access to financing, land, seeds, fertilizers, poultry, agricultural tools, and other necessary resources and production equipment on loan, enabling immigrants to engage in livestock farming. The government will subsidize the company's invested capital with an annual interest rate of 6% to complete the immigration policy. Currently, the 800,000 *cho* (unit of area) of land owned by the East Asia Development Company is being used as a foundation. The plan is to immigrate 2,000 families in the next fiscal year, providing each family with a loan for 20 *cho* of land for cultivation. The first phase will last for ten to fifteen years, during which every effort will be made to complete the project. If the Colonial Affairs Committee approves the company proposal, a founding committee will be established, and the support of private financial groups will be sought to promote its realization. (8th, Japanese United Press)

Development of North China: Japanese Factions in Opposition 29

(Tokyo) Finance Minister Takahashi returned to Tokyo yesterday and will go to the Ministry of Finance tomorrow to begin reviewing the budget for the next fiscal year. The issue of investment and development in North China will be raised again for discussion. Finance Minister Takahashi advocates a gradual approach. On the North China development issue, there are two opposing factions in the Japanese government and financial circles. According to the *Yomiuri Shimbun*, the gradualist faction, with financial capitalists, elder statesmen, the Central Department of the Army, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs as its background, advocates focusing on profitability, prioritizing agriculture over heavy industry, and reducing the financial burden. The rapid development faction, with the Kwantung Army and the South Manchuria Railway as its background, advocates prioritizing national policy over profit, prioritizing mining development and the construction of railways and ports, and prioritizing heavy industry. Civilian fascists and military industrialists support this view. If there is world peace, the gradualist faction will naturally remain dominant. However, if the Italian-Ethiopian war breaks out, the influence of fascist forces will rise, and the rapid development faction will naturally prevail. Therefore, the development of North China will depend on the changing world situation. (8th, China United Press)

Page 7

Anglo-Italian Actions Forming a Mediterranean Hegemony Scenario: Italian Navy Plans Large-Scale Exercises, Britain Dispatches Fleet as Precaution 30

(Rome) The Italian Navy today plans to conduct large-scale exercises in the Eastern Mediterranean. This action is nothing less than a challenge to Britain's historical hegemony in the Mediterranean. It is reported that the most noteworthy aspect of this exercise is the performance of 60 submarines between Sicily and Italian Libya. This submarine force could potentially blockade all traffic in the Mediterranean, cutting off Britain's commercial and naval routes to India, the Far East, and Australia. Observers today believe that if international sanctions are ever implemented, Italy will likely impose a submarine blockade in the Eastern Mediterranean. The exercises will be held in the sea surrounding Malta, which is a crucial base for Britain's trade routes to Suez, Egypt, and India. Traditionally, Britain controls the Strait of Gibraltar. Today, according to reliable sources, Italy is prepared to engage Britain with seven heavy cruisers, twelve light cruisers, fifty-five destroyers, seventy submarines, and forty-five patrol boats. In addition, ten cruisers will soon be completed, totaling 139,000 tons. Adding this to the existing tonnage, the total will reach 455,000 tons. (7th, National Press)

Gibraltar Port: The British battleship "Barham" (27,500 tons) arrived here yesterday from Plymouth. It was originally scheduled to stay for a month, but has now been ordered to sail immediately to Malta. (7th, Havas)

(London) Britain's deployment of its fleet in the Mediterranean is, to some extent, due to the international situation and the need to take precautionary measures, and not purely for autumn maneuvers. This has recently been acknowledged by political figures. The majority of the Mediterranean fleet will be anchored in Alexandria and Port Said in Egypt, and Haifa in Palestine (a British mandate) until October 11. Alexandria and Port Said control the Suez Canal, while Haifa is the terminal of the Iraqi Mosul oil pipeline (this oil pipeline, 1,200 miles long and costing £10 million, was completed in January of this year). The fleet deployment schedule is as follows: (1) Alexandria will be anchored by the 30,000-ton battleships "Warspite" and "Revenge," and the Second Cruiser Squadron (including "London," "Devonshire," and "Shropshire," each with a displacement of 9,500 tons) until September 20. At that time, they will be replaced by the 6th Division of the 3rd Destroyer Flotilla and the 7th Division of the 4th Destroyer Flotilla until September 30. They will then be replaced by the 3rd Cruiser Squadron (including "Arethusa," "Danae," and "Delhi," each with a displacement of 4,850 tons), another cruiser, "Sussex," and the 8th Division of the 4th Destroyer Flotilla. (2) Port Said will be anchored by the 30,000-ton battleship "Resolution" and the cruiser "Arethusa" until September 20. At that time, they will be replaced by the battleship "Revenge" and the 8th Division of the 4th Destroyer Flotilla. (3) Haifa will be anchored by the 8th Division of the 4th Destroyer Flotilla until September 20. At that time, they will be replaced by the Cyprus Reserve Fleet and the cruisers "Devonshire" and "Shropshire" until October 10. They will then be replaced by the cruisers "London" and "Australia" and the 4th Destroyer Flotilla. The battleship "Warspite" will also be anchored in Jaffa (in British-mandated Palestine) from September 20 to September 30. All of the above ships are scheduled to join the other units of the Mediterranean Fleet in a concentrated exercise off the coast of Navarino, Greece, from October 20 to 23, before returning to Malta. Taken together, it is clear that the British Navy can blockade the entrance to the Suez Canal until October 11 and control the sea route from Italy to East Africa in the area of 22 degrees East longitude until October 23. (7th, Havas)

League of Nations Special Committee Begins Work, Urges Italy and Ethiopia to Moderate Tone, British and French Members Offer New Contributions, Hoping for Swift Resolution Plan 31

(Geneva) The Committee of Five today sent a telegram to the Italian and Ethiopian governments, asking them to moderate their tone during the negotiations and to avoid actions that would make the committee's work difficult. The committee has decided to create a new mediation plan based on the recommendations of the Paris conference. It is said that the Ethiopian representative has requested that the committee complete its work within a week. Laval will return to Paris this afternoon after the Committee of Five meeting, fearing that he will not be able to attend the League of Nations Assembly in person, so he will appoint Herriot and Boncour as the French representatives. (7th, National Press)

(Geneva) French Prime Minister Laval, as a member of the special Committee of Five, is now advocating the establishment of a gendarmerie in Ethiopia, commanded by British and Italian officers, to resolve the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. However, this proposal has not yet been submitted for discussion. There is also a proposal to allow Italy to establish military camps and airfields in Ethiopia, following the example of Britain in Iraq. However, the British military presence in Iraq is purely to protect the route to India and does not interfere in the country's local affairs. If the Italian military were to be stationed in Ethiopia, the benefits it would receive would be comparable to those of the British in Iraq. It is not yet known when the Committee of Five's report will be drafted, but all members advocate proceeding with everything as quickly as possible to avoid delays. At the same time, the League of Nations Assembly will open tomorrow, and the Secretary-General's report will inevitably address the Ethiopian case. So far, Italy has not indicated that if the Ethiopian representatives attend the Assembly, the Italian representatives will be unwilling to attend. (8th, Reuters)

(Geneva) This morning, the League of Nations Council held a public meeting to discuss various non-political issues. After about half an hour, it immediately discussed the matters secretly discussed in the Committee of Five on Abyssinia. Eden first described the results of the Paris tripartite conference and his contributions to Italy at that time. It is said that Eden's report to the Committee of Five was much more detailed, due to its confidentiality, than the report he gave in the public meeting. (7th, National Press)

(Geneva) People here now feel that the League of Nations Council's second week of work will not be as difficult as its initial meeting. Although no one dares to be optimistic, the crisis has been temporarily preserved. Italy has not changed its attitude, but it does not seem to oppose the Council's procedures and seems prepared to discuss any reasonable proposals made to Italy. This will only progress after the Committee of Five submits its report. As for when the committee will provide its report, it is not yet possible to predict, but it is said that the proceedings are not allowed to be delayed. As for Ethiopia, if its independence seems guaranteed, it is likely to resist. As for Italy, Mussolini has stated his views and will not take hostile action during the discussion. The Italian representative, Aloisi, will handle any proposals that the Committee of Five may put forward with agility. However, the season for military action in East Africa is approaching, and it is expected that Mussolini will not let this opportunity pass. French Prime Minister Laval has gone to Paris and will return to Geneva on Tuesday. However, the Committee of Five will reconvene tomorrow afternoon. One of the main demands put forward by the Italian government is the security of its colonial borders. The borders of the British and French colonies, which are adjacent to the Ethiopian border, are longer than Italy's, but they do not feel the need to protect their security. However, given the atmosphere that has already been created between Italy and Ethiopia, this Italian demand must be given appropriate consideration. The League of Nations believes that the establishment of an international gendarmerie, led by neutrals such as people from the Scandinavian Peninsula, would provide the security that Italy needs. However, Italy has already rejected such proposals. (8th, Reuters)

Ciano's Speech Targeted at the United States: Willing to Exert Every Effort Against Anyone Obstructing Italy's Historical Progress, No Peaceful Cooperation Between Italy and Ethiopia Possible 32

Asmara, Eritrea: Mussolini's son-in-law, Count Ciano, former Italian ambassador to China, broadcast a speech here, directed specifically at the Americans. Ciano said that the Italian people are prepared to use all possible means, even to the extreme, to resist those who attempt to harm Italy and obstruct the course of history. He then elaborated that although the rulers of Ethiopia are perfidious and hostile to Italy, Italy has still been willing to make compromises in an attempt to achieve peaceful cooperation with Ethiopia, but this has ultimately been unsuccessful. The Ethiopian authorities have done everything in their power to disrupt the peace of Africa outside their borders in an attempt to prevent the economic control of abundant markets by the civilized world. To take this action in a world already affected by serious hardship is a crime. All friends of peace in Africa and the world will now know the futility of discussing sanctions and other methods aimed at curbing Italy's ambitions. Italy has now decided that it will no longer attempt to achieve peaceful cooperation with Ethiopia and will not accept any empty promises, given Ethiopia's past failure to keep its word. Today, a large army is gathered in Eritrea, with everyone of one mind. At the sound of the Prime Minister's command, everyone is willing to fight to the death. All those who bear the responsibility for this particularly important decision in world history must not forget that 43 million Italians are now motivated by a single religion, willing to safeguard Italy's future strength in Mussolini's name, regardless of the cost or the number of opponents. After Ciano's speech, he and Mussolini's two sons flew in a plane to scout the situation of the Ethiopian army. Ciano is currently Minister of Propaganda and holds the rank of Captain in the Air Force and he and Mussolini’s two sons are currently serving in Africa. (8th, Reuters)

U.S. Chargé d'Affaires Statement: Maintaining Friendship with Ethiopia, Abandoning Oil Rights for the Sake of Peace 33

Addis Ababa: U.S. Chargé d'Affaires Van Nierkirk recently met with the Emperor to inform him that the U.S. decision to cancel the oil concession was solely to maintain international peace and that U.S. friendship with Ethiopia has not changed in the slightest. It should be noted that after the cancellation of the oil concession, the Ethiopian people expressed dissatisfaction. (7th, Havas)

Italy's Minimum Conditions: Military Occupation of Ethiopia, Claiming Britain and France Have Precedent to Cite, Skepticism About Efforts in Geneva 34

(Rome) Prime Minister Mussolini's mouthpiece, *Il Popolo d'Italia*, recently elaborated on the minimum conditions that Italy can accept regarding the Ethiopian issue: "The current international situation must be clearly defined, that is, Ethiopia must be demilitarized and occupied by Italian forces for supervision. As for a sovereign nation being militarily occupied by another country, there is a precedent to cite, such as the presence of British troops in Egypt and China. Britain and France have the responsibility to govern independently and do not allow other countries to interfere. The mandates of various countries, which originally had a collective nature, have gradually become colonies or protectorates. If Britain and France propose a joint aid plan for the Ethiopian issue, rather than allowing Italy to do it alone, it will only lead to disputes." (7th, Havas)

(Rome) Regarding the Ethiopian issue, political figures have once again expressed skepticism about the efforts made by representatives of various countries in Geneva, believing that unless the countries concerned obtain the minimum compromise conditions, the crux of the problem will not be resolved. Recently, direct talks between the leaders of Britain, France, and Italy have been under consideration, but to ensure their success, these minimum conditions are indispensable. The general public believes that the maximum conditions proposed by Britain and France are still far from the minimum conditions that Italy can accept. As far as Italy is concerned, if its security needs are to be guaranteed, then Ethiopia must be brought under its control to be effective. It goes without saying that Italy must respect the interests of Britain and France in Ethiopia. In addition, some left-wing elements in a certain country are currently promoting an anti-fascist movement, which Italian figures strongly disapprove of, saying that the Italian-Ethiopian dispute may become even more obscure as a result. There are also rumors here that if the debate in Geneva regarding the Italian-Ethiopian dispute is influenced by this movement, then Italy will resolutely withdraw from the League of Nations. (7th, Havas)

Important Ethiopian Commanders: Two Depart for the Front Lines, Troops Gather Awaiting Orders 38

One is Grazmatch Gassas, who led his troops from Jinda towards Magale, a major city in Tigray, on the northern front. The other is Ras Nasibu, who is currently traveling from Harar to a location northwest of Jijiga on the southern front. At the same time, it is reported that the Ethiopian authorities are now releasing thieves from prisons in Addis Ababa and sending them to the northern border to strengthen the defensive forces. It is also reported that the Ethiopian King intends to gradually release prisoners for military service. (7th, Reuters)

Addis Ababa: The Ethiopian troops that have already been mobilized, including tribesmen and professional soldiers, have all been supplied with firearms, ammunition, and horses and have separately departed for their designated locations to gather and await orders. All strategically important locations are now guarded by infantry and cavalry. As for people from the agricultural and commercial sectors who have military obligations, the authorities have separately notified them where to gather after the mobilization order is issued. One-tenth of the civil servants in various agencies have been drafted into the army, but officials claim that the general mobilization order will only be issued after a foreign act of aggression begins. The military authorities of the province of Joga recently led 25,000 troops and many warhorses to the capital to have them inspected by the Emperor. (7th, Havas)

Addis Ababa: It was learned today that the Ethiopian King has temporarily postponed the issuance of a general mobilization order for the Ethiopian army to await changes in the situation. However, the chiefs of all tribes across the country have been quietly training their subordinates, indicating that once the mobilization order is issued, 1.25 million people will be ready to serve on the battlefield. Unfortunately, observers say that all the soldiers' weapons are of poor quality. (7th, National Press)

Greece Expands Navy: Invites Bids for Four Additional Destroyers 39

Athens: The government plans to add four destroyers through a bidding process. It has sent notices to various foreign shipyards inviting bids and stipulating that all destroyers ordered must be completed within two years. (8th, Havas)

League of Nations Advisory Committee on Opium: Passes Annual Report, to Be Submitted to the Council for Discussion 40

(Geneva) The League of Nations Advisory Committee on Opium continued its meeting. Chairman Lyall, the British representative, passed the annual report to be submitted to the Council for discussion. The International Convention on Limiting the Manufacture and Regulating the Distribution of Narcotic Drugs, signed in Geneva on July 13, 1931, has been declared ratified by most countries. This year is the first year of implementing this convention. The committee has studied the difficulties encountered in its implementation, believing that the ban on illegal exports stipulated in the convention has achieved satisfactory results. The committee has also studied the fact that large quantities of opium are often diverted to other places for illegal sale before reaching their destination. It has decided to propose to the governments of various countries that, when issuing export licenses to countries that need very little opium and countries that do not re-export opium, strict supervision must be carried out to avoid covert exports. The production of heroin and morphine last year decreased compared to the years before 1933. The committee believes that this achievement can be considered satisfactory. (7th, Havas)

Dignitaries Gather in Geneva: League of Nations Assembly Opens Today, Agenda Includes Five Items, Election of Three Non-Permanent Council Members 41

(Geneva) The League of Nations Annual Assembly is scheduled to open tomorrow and will last for three weeks. The first meeting will be chaired by Argentine representative, Chinchinaga, the chairman of the Council, as usual, who will deliver the opening address. The agenda includes three items: (1) Election of the President of the Assembly, Czech Foreign Minister Benes is expected to be elected. (2) Election of six Vice-Presidents of the Assembly and six Chairmen and several members of various committees. (3) General debate on the activities of the League of Nations, during which the representatives of various countries will likely explain the views of their governments on the Italian-Ethiopian dispute. British Foreign Secretary Hoare will also clarify Britain's position. In addition, the agenda will also include two items: (1) Election of three non-permanent members of the Council to replace Poland, Czechoslovakia, and Mexico, whose terms have expired. Poland is expected to be re-elected, while the other two seats will likely belong to Romania and Colombia. (2) Election of a judge of the Permanent Court of International Justice to replace the late Japanese judge, Adachi. League of Nations officials believe that Nagaoka, the former Japanese ambassador to France, will definitely be elected. Representatives from various countries and journalists have arrived one after another, making the city very lively, and the fine weather has made the excitement even greater. British Foreign Secretary Hoare, French Minister Without Portfolio Herriot, and former Foreign Minister Boncour will arrive here tonight. (8th, Havas)

Minister of Communications Mr. Tokonami Passes Away from Illness; Vacancy Temporarily Filled by Prime Minister; New Party Movement Suffers Setback 42

(Tokyo) Mr. Takejiro Tokonami, the Minister of Communications, had been suffering from nephritis and catarrh of the trachea and bronchi since mid-July. He had been recuperating at his residence in Nishi-Okubo, Yodobashi Ward, but suddenly developed a severe case of cardiac paralysis around 6:00 AM on the 8th, becoming critically ill. He passed away at 6:40 AM, at the age of 70. (United Press dispatch of the 8th)

(Tokyo) Born in the second year of the Keio era, he was a member of the samurai class of Kagoshima. In the 22nd year of the Meiji era, he graduated from the political science department of the Imperial University. He successively held positions such as Secretary of the Ministry of Finance, Director of the Ehime Prefecture Tax Bureau, Councilor of Miyagi Prefecture, Secretary of Niigata and Akita Prefectures, Governor of Tokushima and Akita, Director of the Local Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Home Affairs, Vice-Minister of Home Affairs, and President of the Railway Board. In the seventh year of the Taisho era, when the Hara Cabinet was formed, he was appointed Minister of Home Affairs. Afterwards, as a leader of the political party, he was highly regarded. He entered the cabinet several times. In July of the ninth year of the Showa era, when the Okada Cabinet was formed, he left the Seiyukai party and joined the cabinet as Minister of Communications, forming the "elder statesmen" group with Prime Minister Okada, Finance Minister Takahashi, and Commerce Minister Machida. (Dentsu dispatch of the 8th)

The Late Japanese Minister of Communications, Takejiro Tokonami

(Tokyo) Due to the death of Minister of Communications Tokonami, Prime Minister Okada has decided to concurrently serve as Minister of Communications. The imperial appointment ceremony will be held at the Hayama Imperial Villa at 10:00 AM tomorrow. (Dentsu dispatch of the 8th)

(Tokyo) Machida, the president of the Minseito party, met with advisor Wakatsuki today, and then visited Prime Minister Okada at 3:00 PM to recommend Takukichi Kawasaki as the successor to Minister of Communications Tokonami. According to Machida, it has been decided to have the Prime Minister temporarily hold the post concurrently, but this cannot continue for long. A decision should be made within the next two days. (United Press dispatch of the 8th)

(Tokyo) Vice-Minister of Communications Oohashi recently told reporters the following: "For the Ministry of Communications, at this time of formulating the budget for the next fiscal year, the Minister is especially important for the implementation of important national policy plans regarding the promotion of civil aviation, wireless telegraph and telephone services, Sino-Japanese telegraph and telephone services, submarine telegraph cables, and other national policies. Especially regarding the promotion of civil aviation, the Minister intended to personally guide the matter after recovering from his illness, and planned to meet with Finance Minister Takahashi at the end of this month to engage in political negotiations. Now that things have come to this, the Minister's passing is truly a major blow to the Ministry of Communications in implementing the aforementioned policies." (United Press dispatch of the 8th)

(Tokyo) The funeral of the late Minister of Communications Tokonami is scheduled for 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 11th at the Aoyama Cemetery, and will be a Shinto-style farewell ceremony. Prime Minister Okada will be the chairman of the funeral committee, and Keisuke Mochizuki and Marquis Toshiitake Ookubo will serve as vice-chairmen. (Dentsu dispatch of the 8th)

(Tokyo) Minister of Communications Tokonami, who passed away, had been recuperating at his residence in Yodobashi since the beginning of July. He ultimately succumbed to old age and his severe asthma, coupled with heart fatigue. However, the Minister's death is significant because it comes just as the budget for the next fiscal year is being compiled and the political season is approaching. The Seiyukai defectors such as Agriculture Minister Yamazaki and Tetsusho Utida deeply fear that this matter will affect politics, so they outwardly feign optimism. However, if this were a party cabinet, the Minister of Communications would have already been replaced. Furthermore, the plan to establish a new party has suffered a setback due to Tokonami's death, and the Seiyukai can breathe a little easier. However, the actions of the Tokonami faction within the Seiyukai are quite noteworthy. (Dentsu dispatch of the 8th)

(Tokyo) The sudden death of Minister of Communications Tokonami has caused considerable panic within the Tokonami faction of the Seiyukai, and they are currently discussing countermeasures. Although the Tokonami faction is within the Seiyukai, they often collaborated with the three cabinet members of the Okada Cabinet, adopting an attitude of maintaining the current cabinet. Therefore, they were often subjected to retaliation as heretics within the party. Now that Mr. Tokonami has passed away, although they can still collaborate with Ministers Yamazaki and Utida, the extent of that collaboration will be very limited. Therefore, their relationship with the current cabinet will also be diminished. Currently, the only option for the members of the Asariso group is to return to the Seiyukai. On the Seiyukai side, the passing of Minister of Communications Tokonami will reduce the splinter groups within the party and promote the strengthening of party unity. However, after Mr. Tokonami's death, the Seiyukai's bases in Kyushu and other places will inevitably be subject to considerable encroachment by various factions. From this perspective, the troubles under this meaning will also increase considerably. (United Press dispatch of the 8th)

Full Text of Correspondence Between US President and Mr. Howard; Greatly Affects the Future of the New Deal 43

(Washington) The recent correspondence between President Roosevelt and Mr. Howard, the chairman of the Howard newspaper company, has a great impact on the future of the New Deal in the United States. The original text is recorded as follows:

Letter from Howard to the President

Your Excellency President Roosevelt,

As an independent editor, I pay close attention to the goals of the New Deal, and also strive to understand why the business community is hesitant and opposed to your plans, while the general electorate has no complaints. I do not believe that the interests of the business community must conflict with the interests of the general public. Although I cannot fully agree with your views on specific issues, I do agree with your interpretation of American liberalism. Therefore, I respectfully present my humble opinions in a friendly and constructive spirit as follows: The attitude of some members of the business community towards the current government is already obvious. If these members are all financial tyrants who specialize in enriching themselves at the expense of the public interest, then there is no need to pay attention to them. Unfortunately, the national business community, which sincerely supported Your Excellency in the past, has now turned to fear, and is not only opposed. Currently, there is no shortage of loyal people who deeply feel that the new taxes advocated by Your Excellency are retaliation against the business community, rather than a plan for national revenue. They deeply feel that the government is trying to avoid expanding the scope of tax collection, and feel that if the government cannot give industry a chance to catch its breath, slightly suspend experimental policies, so that the country can recover its losses and the business community can reduce its fear, then there will be no true recovery. Your Excellency has repeatedly stated your position on various national issues, so I do not hesitate to repeat myself again. Those who misunderstand the New Deal have caused a lot of damage. Your Excellency and I both know that although our national system has various errors, the achievements in the past have enabled us to achieve more progress than any other system in the world. Therefore, Your Excellency should quickly dispel the saying that confuses the public, that orderly reform is a disguised revolution.

Howard

President Roosevelt's Reply to Mr. Howard

Mr. Howard,

Your letter is very impressive. Your suggestions are based on your observations of the country's situation and are deeply appreciated. I am also well aware that Congress has passed many bills after a long period of meetings, which inevitably cause some people to feel confused.

Criticism is Inevitable

I can ignore the critics, as no one who has never governed can avoid criticism. I can also ignore others who have partisan biases or specialize in harming others for their own benefit. There are still people who want the government to be quiet and inactive. These people already had this idea when former Presidents Roosevelt and Wilson were in office. The people of the country also know what the meaning of this kind of opposition is.

Accepting Criticism

However, in addition to this, there are sincere and fair criticisms, and I am willing to work with the government to discuss them. I will naturally clarify the government's purpose, explain the government's methods, restate the government's ideals, and the unbiased news media, which cares about the public welfare and publishes impartial news, will also be helpful to the government's efforts.

Dispelling Concerns

Experience is the best teacher, and results are the best evidence. Therefore, if we briefly describe the government's past measures, we can dispel all concerns, and the entire business community will later agree with our point of view, that the interests of the business community do not conflict with the interests of the entire people, but are in harmony with each other. In general, economic decline is the accumulation of unsound organization in agriculture, commerce, and finance.

Legislative Relief

Our legislation was created to relieve this phenomenon, so it cannot be analyzed as either recovery or reform. Our actions are all based on the fundamental economic principles set three years ago. At that time, I said that the economic life of the American people should be balanced, the people's trust in the banking system should be restored, the interests of investors in the securities market should be protected, the labor community should have the freedom to organize and be free from exploitation, the country's rich resources should be protected and developed, the elderly and unemployed should have social security, poverty should be alleviated, and investors and consumers should reduce the burden of superfluous companies. I do not believe that any responsible political party dares to publicly oppose any of the above goals.

Tax Plan

As for the tax plan you mentioned, it is based on a broad and fair socioeconomic goal. This goal is not to destroy wealth, but to create a wider range of opportunities, to prevent unsound accumulation, and to place the government's heavy responsibility on those who are most capable of shouldering it. Therefore, those affected are only individuals with an annual income of more than $50,000 and estates exceeding $40,000. It is also a recognized fact that large companies have a greater tax-paying capacity than small companies. Anyone who knows a little bit about the matter will not think that this kind of tax will harm the entire business community. Moreover, after the new law was established, it has slightly reduced the corporate tax rate by 95 percent. If it is said that a small amount of excess profits tax, etc., can encourage the simplification of company organization. Congress did not allow the scope of tax collection to be expanded, because Congress recognized that it has already been expanded a lot in the past five years. During the discussion, they even used the United Kingdom as an example, arguing that American citizens, everyone (missing characters), the expansion of the tax scope in recent years has all been indirect taxes, so that the poor bear a heavier burden. For example, in 1929, various consumption taxes only accounted for 30% of government revenue, but today they account for 60%. Even after the recent tax bill is passed, it will only reduce by half a percent.

Caution is Best

At the beginning of the current government's administration, there was an expanded legislative plan, and it was known that the domestic situation required drastic action. However, Congress and I both felt that caution was best, so that the business community and the general public could understand where the reform was. Now the fundamental procedures have been largely completed, and the opportunity for a breather that you mentioned is already here.

Unremitting Efforts

The current domestic situation has greatly improved, and the future of recovery will naturally be easier to advance. Although unemployment has not been completely eliminated, it has gradually decreased, and the government's efforts to solve the unemployment problem have not been reduced. I dare not claim to have the means of a magician, nor dare I claim that the improvement of the environment is entirely due to the government's efforts, but I know that the government's various measures have indeed helped to restore people's self-confidence.

Roosevelt (National Telegram of the 7th)

When the plane crashed, she jumped out of the plane, but still hit a tree and died. The pilot, Captain Stewart of London, died in the destroyed plane. The fire was extinguished by the Economic Defense Team. When the plane crashed, debris hit a woman walking on the road, and she also died instantly. The other plane that was hit, although heavily damaged, still landed safely, and the pilot was unharmed. When the accident occurred, thousands of vacationers were watching, and they were all greatly shocked. (Reuters dispatch of the 7th)
