Shen Bao Local Supplement

Casual Talk

Three of Diplomatic Means 197

— Shun

Large-scale maneuvers and large-scale exchanges are a kind of armed demonstration and have nothing to do with diplomatic means. Diplomatic means are used to resolve international disputes with non-military means, so they are called diplomatic means. However, diplomatic means are not used with military force as a backing. No matter how flexible your means are, they will definitely not have any effect. This is an iron rule taught by history and cannot be denied.

When the situation in the Far East was urgent, the United States also had a large-scale maneuver in the Pacific, but it did not reverse the already bad situation. Therefore, simply conducting large-scale maneuvers to intimidate cannot have any diplomatic impact. Now that the Italian-Ethiopian War is about to break out, although the United Kingdom, France, and other countries have tried their best to mediate, there is no hope for a peaceful resolution. Furthermore, after the oil concession in Ethiopia was granted to the Fil Oil Exploration Company, it further aroused the anger of the Italians. Although the US government has expressed its intention to give up, the Ethiopian government and the company still do not want to give up. Therefore, once the Italian-Ethiopian War suddenly breaks out, it is still unknown whether it will not lead to an expansion of the situation. Therefore, when "the mountain rain is about to come and the wind fills the building" today, the European powers cannot help but have a frowning expression, as if a great disaster is about to come. It can be seen that diplomatic means are not enough to open the difficult situation of the Italian-Ethiopian dispute.

According to a Rome dispatch on the 25th of last month, the Italian military's large-scale maneuvers began. The army was about 500,000 people, and the hypothetical enemy invaded from the German-Austrian border to test the combat strength of the mechanized army. According to a London dispatch on the 30th, the United Kingdom launched diplomatic and military forces to cope with serious events in the future. The Mediterranean fleet was very busy with deployments. According to a London dispatch on the 2nd, Italy's large-scale maneuvers in the northern territory have now ended, and the United Kingdom, France, and Germany will follow up with large-scale maneuvers to show their military strength. Large-scale maneuvers by the French army have already begun on the border between Qu and Conde, and at the same time, Germany has begun to hold the first public performance of mock war exercises since the establishment of the Treaty of Versailles. As for the British army, it will go to Salisbury Plain to create the thirteenth mock war exercise. Originally, this kind of mock war exercise cannot be regarded as the prelude to the Second World War, but at least it can be regarded as a way to seek the smooth progress of diplomacy.

According to a Geneva dispatch on the 5th, the League of Nations Administrative Council, which had the last hope for peace, held a meeting, and the future showed ominous signs. The Ethiopian representative spoke eloquently, and the Italian representative left the meeting in anger. Although British and French diplomats used all kinds of diplomatic methods to eliminate the war between Italy and Ethiopia, they have come to an end. At this point, it is feared that there will be no possibility of using diplomatic means to resolve the difficult situation in the future. Only by using strength to resolve the current difficulties, the outcome of the war, and who will win, can only be proved by the results of the war in the future.

Mountain Village Rainy Night 198

— Lin Xi

Returning from the city, it was evening. We planned to rush back to the mountain before dark, but we hadn't even gone halfway when it started to rain. We urged the mule driver to run fast, and we reached a town seven or eight miles away from the mountain, and our clothes were soaked. We had dinner at a small shop, dried our clothes by the fire, rested our feet, hoping that the rain would stop so we could rush back to the mountain, but the rain seemed to be getting heavier and heavier, as if it was deliberately making things difficult for us.

It was getting dark, and the wind was blowing the rain against the window of the small shop. The small reed curtain rolled up and fell down again regardless. The window paper was already soaked through. The small shop was pitifully small, and there were no larger shops in the small town for the three of us to spend the night. Just watching the rain fall was definitely not a solution, so we bought an umbrella—the only one in a salt shop—and braved the rain to rush back to the mountain along the mountain road seven or eight miles away. It had been too dry for too long, so the rain was particularly heavy. The rainwater on the mountain poured down like small rivers, and we waded in the rivers and rushed along the mountain road.

The darkness was terrifying, and the thunder seemed to be ringing right under our feet, and the lightning was flashing right above us. In the flash of lightning, we saw the dense rain sweeping the mountains and trees with the mountain wind. The small paper umbrella could hardly support it anymore. Against the mountain wind, it was hard to barely block some of the coarse raindrops, and its effectiveness was naturally pitifully small! We were soaked to the skin, and our soaked leather shoes were squeaking. Behind us, our spines and clothes were stuck together. Except for one heart, the whole body was cold.

I was very scared, and I thought of the story of the mountain wolf. At this time, one person's strength is really no match for a wild beast. There wasn't a single sign on the mountain to prove that people lived there! (If there was a lamp in the mountain rain, even if it was a strange will-o'-the-wisp, we would feel at ease!) We were no different from a team of explorers, desperately seeking a place to stay on a stormy night, but there was none. It was a desolate mountain, an isolated island; the momentum of the wind and rain placed us on the black giant waves in the ocean. I had this experience: the dark, gloomy waves rose and fell, like a group of ferocious giant beasts about to devour people; who knew what terrible things were under the waves! I understand the primitive people's worship of nature. I blessed myself and quickened my pace. Everything was sacrificed as expected. The umbrella unfortunately touched a tree branch, broke a big hole, and broke a few ribs, and could no longer hold up, so we simply threw it away, let the rain pour on us, and walked hand in hand.

The big mountain stream that we were most afraid of was in front of us. Our residence was to be reached by crossing this stream. In normal times, the mountain stream was a road, and donkeys and camels could pass through it. But when it rained, the situation was different. This was the most dangerous place: boom! boom! boom! The mountain water poured straight down, carrying branches, weeds, and rocks. We saw the speed of the water flow in a flash of lightning—how terrible! We thought of the safety of our lives. If we were unlucky enough to encounter a large mountain rock rolling down with the current, we would be finished! "A big rock, climb slowly!" I issued a warning as the vanguard. In order to climb, hands and eyes lost contact, and what replaced contact was sound; what a tense sound it was, a cry for survival!

After climbing over the large mountain rock and gasping for breath, we found ourselves in the rushing rapids. What we were treading on under our feet was no longer the familiar road, but an unexpected unevenness: a pit, a small pool, a rock; some of the rocks were still covered with slippery moss, which must have rolled down from the high shady place of the mountain stream. "Hold your hands tight, hold your hands tight," said the smallest male, boom! boom! boom! It was thunder, and the aftersound was still vibrating in the mountainside. The male fell into the turbulent flow! Above his head was a huge thunderbolt, and under his feet he had stepped into a terrible hole—a deep pit, he fell! We picked him up, and I touched his chest: thud, thud! thud! We couldn't help but laugh. "It's almost there, we'll be there after we cross the stream," I comforted him.

Thank goodness! When we looked back at the terrible mountain stream, we couldn't help but shout! How terrible it was: a lightning bolt, a thunderbolt, a torrent of rushing water!

"Hum! A useless umbrella!" After climbing up the mountain stream, we laughed! Don't get sick, I bless us. I asked about the things we brought back from the city, and everyone shook their empty hands and laughed!

When we went to bed, we could still hear the roaring of the mountain stream!

Victims Under Heavy Burdens 199

— Zaishi

He, —a poverty-stricken farmer— struggled to maintain his poor life every year with a few acres of rented fields. The environment bestowed on him every year was like this. There was simply no time for him to be slightly more prosperous. He was unable to improve his life, it could also be said that he did not think of improving his life, and it could even be said that he did not want to improve his life. He only held the mentality that this was a responsibility given to him by heaven, and he was indeed a faithful believer in fatalism; therefore, although he worked hard all day and all year round, he did not have any resentment, no thoughts, and no envy for the beautified lives of the rich. In short: China's unique national character—patience—completely occupied his entire mind.

The food for his wife and children, the losses from fertilizer, etc., the heavy burden of this life, pressed on him, often making him feel panicked. Although there were plenty of longevity granaries in the towns, he was not qualified to step into the door of these longevity granaries. Therefore, borrowing at high interest rates was his only means of salvation. When it came time for the harvest, paying rent and repaying debts was just enough to dispose of all his harvest. He spent a year of labor, the help of his wife and children, and the price he got was just empty hands. So he returned to the life of borrowing to make ends meet. Year after year, he did not feel pain because of the heavy burden of life, and even seemed very satisfied. Patience was his will; fate was his self-comfort.

Even more admirable: he was not willing to relax his responsibility even slightly, that is to say: he was not willing to give up his profit even slightly. He saw that there was a vacant lot next to his house, which could be used to plant small crops, so after some hard work, he implemented his plan and planted a lot of watermelons. In his mind, he only hoped to get some extra income to make up for his losses. This year made him particularly excited. The watermelons on this vacant lot were so abundant. He was full of joy, loaded two large loads of watermelons, and on that morning, carrying this heavy burden of 200 pounds, he rushed to the town ten miles away from his home to sell them. His mood was pleasant. He really wanted to satisfy his hope. At that time, the sun was majestically shining on the earth, and he ran for many miles under this scorching sun, gradually feeling tired. However, he did not take fatigue as pain, but rather as joy. Because he understood that the hotter the weather, the higher the value of watermelons. Unfortunately, just as he was about to reach the town, God suddenly bestowed a heavy rain, soaking his body and mind, drenching him like a drowned chicken. Although he was a very healthy farmer, he could not withstand such destruction, so the source of the disease was sown like this. When he arrived in the town, he saw that there were so many companions who had the same encounter and were selling their watermelons at the same low price. The value of the watermelons was so cheap. He suffered this cold rain-like blow, and his heart was so anxious that a mouthful of fresh blood immediately appeared before his eyes. At this time, his overly tired body could no longer support him. So he barely sold the watermelons, dragged his heavy steps, and walked home. It was pitiful that his illness at that time was already so serious.

Now his son has inherited his father's legacy and will continue to live their arduous life endlessly.

School Enrollment 200

— Erlang

It's funny to say, this summer I went to a place to "escape the heat." It was a school, and no one lived there during summer vacation. My friend, who was a school cadre, strongly invited me to live there, saying, "Living in a pavilion room in such hot weather, move to my place, it's cool and quiet." (And "you don't have to pay rent," he didn't say, but I knew.) So, I "escaped the heat" there. Now that school has started, and I have "escaped the heat" enough, I still returned to the pavilion room.

A few days before I was about to leave, their school was busy with student enrollment registration, and a tragicomedy that was both funny and sad happened.

When a group of innocent and lovely elementary school students was surrounding the director of the elementary school department, talking about their lives during the summer vacation, suddenly an old woman flashed in at the door, holding a seven- or eight-year-old child, and cried out, "Sir," tears streaming down her dark eyes, "my little one wants to go to school." The teacher looked surprised, and the children were also surprised. Why cry when you want to go to school? Before the teacher could speak, the old woman said, crying, "His father is dead"—died last month—"the work I do in a day is only enough to eat, where does the little one get the money to go to school? I wanted to ask him to apprentice at the blacksmith shop, but he's too young, only seven years old, only seven years old. It's better to let him go to school. If he recognizes a few words in the future, when he's ten, study for two years, and ask him to go to a foreign goods store as a student, he'll recognize words and have a chance to stand out. Let him go to school, but there's no money at home... Sir, his father died last month, and there's really no money at home, please do a good deed, sir."... She said a lot, and I, who was listening nearby, didn't know what she meant, and the children didn't understand it even more, but saw her tears and snot just flowing, and she used her sleeves to wipe her nose while talking. The teacher understood, and asked, "You mean, you want it for free? You don't have to pay money, right?" She didn't understand the phrase "for free," but "you don't have to pay money" was it. She said, "Please do a good deed, sir, there's really no money at home. His father..." And she went on and on. The teacher frowned and smiled, and after a long time, he said, "The school also doesn't have much funding, and there's no precedent for free... However, your child's grades were good last semester, he's willing to study hard, and he follows the rules. If you don't have money at home, then... then... I'll discuss it with the principal." She thought the teacher had agreed, and before the teacher could prevent it, she knelt on the ground and kowtowed, saying, "You're doing a good deed, sir,... the little one will have a chance to stand out in the future, all thanks to your kindness." The teacher immediately stood up from the chair, bent down to ask her to get up, "I don't deserve it, I don't deserve it,... I still have to discuss it with the principal," but she only cared about talking and kowtowing, and didn't hear what the teacher said. After kowtowing many times, she stood up on her own, and said with tears, "I still have to work, the little one will come to school today," and ordered the little one she was holding, "Thank you, sir!" meaning that he should also kowtow, but the little one only bowed to the teacher at school, and had never kowtowed before. He looked at his mother, looked at the teacher, and then bowed deeply to the teacher three times. "Kowtow, Xiaoliuzi!" Mom was not satisfied with the three bows, and the little one argued, "The teacher doesn't let people kowtow, he likes bowing." The teacher said, "Bowing is good," and Mom didn't insist, just saying, "Sir, the little one will come to school today, I still have to work," led the little one to the teacher, made a deep bow, and left.

That teacher turned around and said to me, "This semester, there's more than just her requesting for free. The school's economy hasn't increased, and education is also in a slump now." Because I was just moved by the old woman's actions, I said sympathetically, "For someone like her who has upward mobility, and her son is willing to study hard and has good grades, he should be given it for free." The teacher replied, "Children's education should be free in the first place. But public schools still have to charge fees, and private schools, what can be done! Many students are not going to school this semester, because their families don't have money. Alas, it's Children's Year, but fewer children are going to school!" The teacher also became sentimental.

Fraser Street 201

— From Long

After dinner, Brother Zhixiang stepped out of the shop and went to the back of the warehouse to wash his oily body. He immediately felt relaxed and cool, as if he had drunk a glass of water. All the gloominess of the day in 　　州

Page 23

had faded away. So, he moved a stool and sat next to the "glass" door, staring blankly, gazing slowly at the calm, waveless, emerald green sea in the distance.

Arriving in this foreign land for the first time, everything that caught his eye felt new and strange: people were of all shapes and sizes, like at a race exhibition. Some were as black as burnt charcoal, some as white as the rice flour used for making kueh during festivals. When they spoke, it was gibberish, not a single word was understandable, like little rats on the roof beams at home conspiring to steal vegetables, how interesting. Even the water in the harbor was more turquoise and clearer than the water in the ponds back home. The sky seemed a little higher, and clearer too. Moreover, the floating clouds drifting across the blue sky seemed particularly light and agile. "The scenery and landscapes of this foreign land are much more beautiful than back home!" Brother Zhixiang thought to himself. However, when he thought that he had been in this foreign land for a whole month and hadn't found a job, and that he had been rejected at job interviews with people shaking their heads and sighing, "The market is sluggish, it's hard to say if we can even get through the end of the year," he had no choice but to come to his distant uncle's shop to "bum around and eat." During the day, he helped out with chores in the shop.

Gusts of light evening breeze swept across the sky, stirring up layers of brocade-like ripples on the turquoise sea. The coconut groves standing by the harbor whispered softly, like the murmurings of lovers.

"Zhixiang, what's up? Sitting here like a fool... Little guy, homesick again!" Old Du, who was "shipping goods" at the shop, walked over, patted him on the shoulder, and said in a hoarse voice, "Don't be silly, let's go out for a stroll, come with me and chase after some flirtatious whores."

Old Du was a thoroughbred foreigner. According to him, he hadn't been back to Tangshan for over a decade. During the day, whenever he had free time, betel leaves were always in his mouth, chewing until his teeth had turned black. In addition, he always liked to wear a pair of Nanyang black silk pants.

They shuffled along in their slippers along the coast towards Beach Road, passing through many unnamed streets and alleys, in a strange hurry, as if they had something urgent to do, not at all like they were out for a stroll. When they reached the front of the Small Hill "Pasar" (market), Brother Zhixiang was already panting like an overworked ox, his shirt soaked with sweat, as if he had been caught in a rainstorm halfway there.

"Where are we going anyway... Old Du, why are you always rushing like this?" He couldn't help but ask, his voice lacking energy because he was too tired from running.

"Why the rush? Little guy, just follow me, I guarantee you'll have a good time!"

So, they continued to shuffle forward.

The night gradually lowered, swallowing the remaining sunset. The streetlights standing by the roadside cast a dim, weak glow, like the tired eyes of a sleepless person. Entering a dark, narrow alley, Old Du turned his head and whispered in Brother Zhixiang's ear with a grin, "We're here!"

This was really unexpected for Brother Zhixiang. This dark alley was like a "Pasar", with all sorts of races. Especially the women whose faces were rouged like monkey butts were dressed quite flirtatiously, leaning in twos and threes next to the doorframes, enticing passersby with silvery laughter.

"Brother Zhixiang, look at this whore, she's not bad looking, especially the dimples on her face!"

"Eh!..." Brother Zhixiang frowned as if recalling something, his head lowered.

The whore didn't dare to raise her head either, seeming a little embarrassed at heart.

"Haha, I thought you were an honest guy, but you've only been here for less than a month and you've already got a 'lover' (partner)!" Old Du also felt a little strange, and teased.

"What are you saying? This prostitute looks familiar. I remember she came on the same ship as me. She said she was coming here to find her husband, how is she a prostitute now?"

"In this kind of market, even a strong man is constantly worrying about not having a bowl of rice to eat. Maybe her husband has lost his job and wandered off somewhere else?... If she doesn't become a prostitute, what else can she do?"

This sorrow of life hurt their hearts, covering them with a layer of gray-black clouds, and they had no mood to stroll around any further.

New Song Introduction 202

Four Sister Flowers

I love the fragrance of plum blossoms, a sprig adorns my glory; this brave leader does not compete with peaches and plums for beauty. (Plum sings)

I love the fragrance of apricot blossoms, a lifetime enjoyed in offering; this beautiful fairy is used to comparing her clothes with purple and crimson. (Apricot sings)

I love the fragrance of orchids, my silk robe can withstand the coolness of dewdrops; this quiet girl is afraid of comparing her length with ordinary flowers. (Orchid sings)

I love the fragrance of lotus flowers, rising from the mud, naturally fragrant; this noble gentleman wishes to make the clear waves his home. (Lotus sings)

Homeland, homeland! The eyes are filled with the wounds of wind and rain! Wounds! Wounds! Yesterday's fresh flowers are today's funerals! (Two flowers sing together) We four sisters do not learn from the ways of flowers. We endure frost and snow, we resist the waves; we rely on our hands to move straight up the battle line of life, not afraid of violent rain and raging wind, we want to let our free flowers bloom. (Four flowers sing together)

Homeland! Homeland! Cannot escape the bleakness of wind and rain! Bleakness! Bleakness! Today the flowers bloom, tomorrow they are buried! (Two flowers sing together) We four sisters do not learn from the ways of flowers. We are not fragrant in spring, we do not wither in autumn; we are evergreen in all seasons, never sad for wind and rain, no matter the vicissitudes of human life, as long as we sisters never forget each other. (Four flowers sing together)

Storytelling 206

Qian Jingzhang Chen Yaxian Karma Record

Guohua (1200) 2:00 PM to 3:00 PM

Opening "Prostitute's Complaint"

Green bamboo wind reflects the jade window. Qin Lou prostitutes sigh sadly. Hate parents for short-sightedness. Greed for flower money forgets nature. Biological daughter. Sold to Pingkang. Sending off the old and welcoming the new with smiling faces. Still have no fixed husband. Sending Zhang Lang and then Li Lang. Going to bed with a husband participates in heaven and earth. But have never worshiped the hall. Two jade arms pillow a thousand people. A little cherry is tasted by ten thousand guests. Last night's wonderful fate with a suave son. Tonight, I met a stupid, vulgar man. There is also a class of stupid Hans. Often garlic and scallions drink sorghum liquor. There is also a class of sad things. I can't avoid taking tonics. Where do children come from to call mother? Thinking back when Mo Suhui met Zishu Ye. Li Shishi was lucky to accompany the Emperor. It is difficult to learn from a flower queen in West Lake. There is no second oil seller. Qin Xiaoguan may not turn Yang back. It is better to repair a little red thread. Sincerely pray and worship Cihang. It is better than a flower queen to be a prostitute.

Movie News

Gugu Grans Connor's New Work "Golden Thread Melody" Premieres in Nanjing on Wednesday Evening 208

Since the rising silver screen diva Gugu G Lansmor was a stunning success, art-loving audiences are looking forward to the premiere of her second creation. Therefore, the work called "Golden Thread Melody" by Gugu in 1935 broke all box office records when it was premiered in New York, USA, which shows that the genius is indeed a genius. Now Nanjing Grand Theater is scheduled to premiere a special show at 9:15 pm next Wednesday, and selected "Bohemian" "aBoheme," a famous song in "Golden Thread Melody" and "Carmen" and "Butterfly Husband" in "Queen of Song's Love Obsession" as preludes. It also added Columbia's five-two music and art day and night, in order to make it a riot of color and a perfect match, to offer to the gentlemen and ladies in Shanghai.
